August 21, 2001


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor.


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"Over the weekend in Florida, six more people bitten by sharks. Six more. Well, since it's Florida, they're still counting. They're not really sure yet."

Jay Leno:

"It was so hot today, Al Gore said, 'Screw the ozone, turn up the damn air conditioner.'" 

Jay Leno:

"It was so hot, Dick Cheney unzipped his chest all the way down to the navel today."

Jay Leno:

"President Bush continuing with the endless vacation that he's on. You know, we need a new holiday in this country. We need 'Take your President to work' day."

Jay Leno:

"Because he doesn't want to set the record for being on vacation longer than any other President in history, Bush announced this week he's ending his month-long vacation three days early. He's coming home three days early. He's coming back August 31st. August 31st is the Friday before Labor Day weekend, isn't it? Huh? So he's coming back to work on Friday, what, knock off early, maybe. Woo! 2:00, 2:30. Then go to Camp David for some R&R."

Jay Leno:

"I think we found the one world leader who works less than Prince Charles."

Jay Leno:

"I was watching our sister station, MSNBC, yesterday, and the lead story on MSNBC was the news that there was nothing new to report in the Gary Condit story. That was the news, that there was nothing new to report. So remember, when there's nothing new to report, NBC will be the station not to report it first."

Jay Leno:

"Actually, just two hours ago, Gary Condit agreed to an interview with Connie Chung on Thursday night. He's going to talk in front of the nation. And I wonder, how did Connie Chung get this? Well, apparently -- remember last week, Connie Chung interviewed Jesse Jackson's mistress? Apparently, she gave her Condit's home number."

Jay Leno:

"The rumor is also that Gary Condit's wife will be there. She doesn't want to be interviewed. No, no, no. It's just from now on, she's gonna be there whenever Gary talks to another woman."

David Letterman:

"Have you seen the new Al Gore? He's wearing a beard. Have you seen Al Gore wearing a beard? He's hoping that the rabbi look will help him next time in Florida."

David Letterman:

"Have you been following the Gary Condit saga? I just found out Gary Condit is hiding out now in Modesto, California. So now he's disappeared. Usually it's just people he's dating that disappear. But now he's actually disappeared."

David Letterman:

"So after months and months and months of dodging the press, he has dropped out of sight and gone into seclusion with his family...no, wait, I'm sorry, that's President Bush."

David Letterman:

"President Bush.says he needs a month off to unwind. Unwind? When the hell does this guy wind?"

David Letterman:

"If you think about it, he might as well be on vacation, because, really, the only thing he has to do yet this year, I guess, is, you know, light the White House Christmas Tree, and then that will be it."

David Letterman:

President Bush "went to Wisconsin, he went to a Harley Davidson factory, and he rode a motorcycle. And I think it's the biggest thing a President has ridden since..."

Craig Kilborn:

"Bill Clinton turned 55 over the weekend. And Bill spent the day with his loved ones and then Hillary popped out of the cake and yelled, 'Got you, fat ass!'"

HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor.


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"How about all these shark attacks off the coast of Florida? It's getting scary. You get the feeling maybe God is still mad about the election, huh?"

"And the day after tomorrow, Gary Condit will be interviewed by Connie Chung on ABC's Primetime Thursday. Ew! Clean the screen for that one, huh?"

Gary Condit's "people said today he was considering giving the interview to Ed Bradley or Stone Phillips, but he decided if you're gonna lie to someone, he's more comfortable doing it with a woman."

"Connie's gonna be alone with him -- 30 minutes with Gary Condit. 30 minutes, alone with him. Sounds like a bad episode of 'Fear Factor,' doesn't it?"

"Actually, at her own station, Connie Chung beat out both Barbara Walters and Diane Sawyer for the interview. She beat them. Well, today, an ABC News spokesman said that both Barbara and Diane are very happy that Connie got it. Boy, you thought Condit was a good liar, huh?"

Jay Leno:

"I just hope Condit makes the interview on time. Remember, he threw his watch in the dumpster."

Jay Leno:

"I'll tell you, though, a lot of interest. Even President Bush is gonna watch. In fact, today, Bush asked a reporter, 'Hey, what night is Primetime Thursday on?'"

Jay Leno:

"President Bush said today he'll return to the White House on August 31st or possibly the 32nd. He's not sure, depending on his schedule."

Jay Leno:

"He's coming home early from his month-long -- who takes a -- besides homeless people, who has a month off?"

Jay Leno:

"Well, today, the White House announced that on August 26th, George W. Bush will become the first President in history to attend the championship game of the Little League World Series. Huh? I see Dick Cheney's finally giving Bush a little more responsibility, huh?"

Jay Leno:

"State police in Philadelphia have arrested a 45-year-old man who beat up Hillary Clinton's brother, Tony Rodham. You know Tony Rodham? He's married to Barbara Boxer's daughter, the senator from California. This guy caught Tony having sex with his girlfriend in a hotel room. Just wailed the guy, just beat him up. And today, Hillary issued a statement saying she is in shock -- shock that her husband Bill was not involved."

Jay Leno:

"See, at least Bill had the class to wait till the husband left the room. You know what I'm saying?"

David Letterman:

"Have you folks been following the Congressman Gary Condit saga? Quite a guy, huh? Piece of work, don't you think? Apparently now he's in seclusion, and he's back in Modesto, and he's rambling around in his big, huge house kind of talking to nobody there, and I said to myself, 'It's like I have a twin.'"

David Letterman:

"Connie Chung will be interviewing Gary Condit, I guess sometime this week. And he set up...here are the rules for the Gary Condit interview. He wants to wear a ski mask. He'll be wearing dark glasses, and will only answer to the name Kurt."

David Letterman:

"But this is all part of Gary Condit trying to make a comeback. He's also going to be appearing on 'Primetime Glick.'"

David Letterman:

"The interview will take place at an undisclosed location. Undisclosed location. Isn't that where his dates usually end up?"

David Letterman:

"Did you hear about Hillary Clinton's brother? It's not Hugh, it's Tony. Did you hear about this story? Apparently he's got, like, a vacation house somewhere in Pennsylvania, and he gets beat up, see? Because he's having sex with somebody's fiance. Yeah, and I'm thinking, boy, this Clinton's a lucky guy, if you think about it, you know what I mean? Really. It's hard to find a brother-in-law who has the same interests as you."

Craig Kilborn:

"Our top story, in C-minus students rule the world, President George W. Bush took time out from his busy vacation schedule to talk to a crowd in Independence, Missouri, at Truman Middle School. . Bush spent most of the day wondering how they knew Harry Truman was going be President when they named the school after him."

Craig Kilborn:

"In the guy who was in charge of the airport in 'Die Hard 2' news, former actor and now Sen. Fred Thompson with the pie in the face treatment from the Tennessee Titans during a visit to training camp. Gary Condit, that is a dignified politician right there."

Jay Leno:

And as the police have already shown us, it takes at least three interviews before Condit even thinks about telling the truth. 30 minutes. I know it doesn't seem like much, but it's still 15 more minutes than he ever spent with his own wife, so that's pretty good."

"And they said the interview will be totally unedited. It's gonna be what they call 'lie to videotape.'"

Jay Leno:

"And no ground rules. ABC said no ground rules for this. No ground rules at all. Unless, of course, Gary gets Connie on the ground. Then they will step in."

Jay Leno:

"Today President Bush announced he's cutting his vacation short by yet another day. Whoo, take a break, fella!"

Jay Leno:

"You know why Bush is coming back two days early now? The fishing hole on his ranch is dried up. See, that's when you know you've been on vacation a long time, okay? When entire bodies of water just start drying up."

Jay Leno:

"And they keep calling this a working vacation. You know, every time you see Bush, he's having fun. He's playing golf. He's riding horses. He's jogging. You know, to everybody else, that's summer camp."

Jay Leno:

"Senator Hillary Clinton's brother Tony Rodham was beaten up by a guy who caught him having sex with his girlfriend. Isn't that great? So it looks like Connie Chung has found next week's interview, huh?"

Jay Leno:

"The guy goes in, beats him up because he's having sex with his girl. See, that's why Hillary has stuck with Bill all these years. He's like a brother to her."

Jay Leno:

"In fact, the cops said Tony Rodham was so swollen from the beating, they thought it was Hugh Rodham."

Jay Leno:

"Well, here's the part where it gets very weird, okay? Tony Rodham is married to the daughter of Barbara Boxer, one of Hillary Clinton's fellow senators. This is like a bad episode of 'Washington, 90201.'"

Jay Leno:

"In Palm Beach on the news today, they were showing people how to fend off a shark attack, how to defend yourself against a shark. Palm beach? Palm beach? These are the same people who, last November, couldn't figure out how to punch a hole."

Jay Leno:

"Al Sharpton says he's going to run for President of the US. I don't know. President Al Sharpton, huh? Good luck getting that giant head on a coin, huh? How are they gonna put that -- you're gonna need a nickel the size of a hubcap now."

Jay Leno:

"The FBI busted a conspiracy that rigged the Monopoly game at McDonald's. Hey, you gotta hand it to the FBI. They might not know how to catch the guy stealing our nuclear secrets, but when it comes to somebody trying to get a free bag of fries - 'Come on! We got him!'"

David Letterman:

"McDonald's, you know, they got some good news today. When Bush found out about them rigging the contest, he said, 'Okay, I'd like you to handle the next election in Florida.'"

David Letterman:

"Thursday night, Connie Chung will interview Gary Condit and then Friday morning, the police will interview Gary Condit. 'Mr. Condit, when was the last time you saw Connie Chung?'"

David Letterman:

"I'm looking forward to the interview. It's been a long time since we've seen a philandering politician hold his wife's hand on TV, you know?"

David Letterman:

"Connie, understandably -- like this is a journalistic coup -- she's very, very excited about it. She's getting ready for the interview. She's got a brand-new outfit, I read. She's got some, like, makeup ready to go. She's got a new can of pepper spray. She's set."

David Letterman:

"President Bush, let's see what the hell is he doing. Oh, he's still on a working vacation. I believe it will come to an end January 20, 2005. That will be it for the working vacation."

David Letterman:

"You know, what a working vacation is? That's where they mix business with pleasure. It's the same kind of thing Clinton used to do at his desk!"

Craig Kilborn:

"President Bush is still on vacation at his ranch. I saw him on a horse in a cowboy hat the other day and I thought what a great country where my President, if he tries hard enough, can grow up to be a little boy."

'Congressman Gary Condit -- for the past 11 years he's worked hard for northern California. If reelected, he will make good on these three promises: He will fight to lower taxes. That's the Condit guarantee. Paid for by the Committee to Reelect Gary Condit.'"
